<script>
$(function(){
	var oSsgViewTranslate = new ssg.View.translate({
		i18nConfig: {
			name:'Messages',
			path:'//ui.ssgcdn.com/ui/ssg/js/i18/front',
			language:'ko',
			mode:'both',
			async: true
		}
	});

	$('#utilLangSelect').on('changeTranslatedGnb', function(event, sDataLang){
		var reactName = '氇瓣车|GNB|り淡_甑';
		if(sDataLang == 'en_US') {
			reactName = '氇瓣车|GNB|り淡_';
		} else if(sDataLang == 'zh_CN') {
			reactName = '氇瓣车|GNB|り淡_欷甑';
		} else {
			reactName = '氇瓣车|GNB|り淡_甑';
		}
		ssg_react.directCall({tarea: reactName})
		location.href = addLocaleParam(sDataLang);
	});

	oSsgViewTranslate.on('reloadTranslated', function(sDataLang) {
		var currentUrl = location.href,
			locale = getLocaleCode(sDataLang),
			localeStr = 'locale=' + locale;
		//changeTranslatedGnb 措菠 氚 挫   reloadTranslated 措菠鸽 氚  瓴届瓣 挫 氚╈挫╉
		//) 欷甑措 氤 措 氤
		if(currentUrl.indexOf(localeStr) < 0) {
			location.href = addLocaleParam(sDataLang);
		}
	});

	function addLocaleParam(sDataLang) {
		var currentUrl = location.href,
			sharpIndex = currentUrl.indexOf('#'),
			paramIndex = currentUrl.indexOf('?'),
			sharpStr = sharpIndex > -1 ? currentUrl.substring(sharpIndex, currentUrl.length) : '',
			urlRemovedSharp = sharpIndex > -1 ? currentUrl.substring(0, sharpIndex) : currentUrl, // '#' 瓯半 url
			urlArray = [],
			baseUrl = '',
			paramStr = '';
			paramArray = [],
			newParamArray = [],
			resultUrl = '',
			locale = getLocaleCode(sDataLang);

		//茧疙瓣  瓴届, #    
		if(paramIndex == -1) {
			resultUrl = urlRemovedSharp + '?locale=' + locale + sharpStr;
			return resultUrl;
		}

		//茧疙瓣  瓴届, #    
		urlArray = urlRemovedSharp.split('?');
		baseUrl = urlArray[0];
		paramStr = urlArray[1];
		//locale 茧疙瓣  瓴届办 locale毵 於臧
		if(paramStr.indexOf('locale') == -1) {
			resultUrl = baseUrl + '?locale=' + locale + '&' + paramStr + sharpStr;
			return resultUrl;
		}

		//locale 茧疙瓣  瓴届 瓯绊瓿 れ 攵
		paramArray = paramStr.split('&');
		for(var x = 0; x < paramArray.length; x++) {
			if(paramArray[x].indexOf('locale') == -1) {
				newParamArray.push(paramArray[x]);
			}
		}
		resultUrl = baseUrl + '?locale=' + locale + (newParamArray.length > 0 ? '&' + newParamArray.join('&') : '') + sharpStr;
		return resultUrl;
	}

	function getLocaleCode(sDataLang) {
		var locale = '';
		if(sDataLang == 'en_US') {
			locale = 'en-US';
		} else if(sDataLang == 'zh_CN') {
			locale = 'zh-CN';
		} else {
			locale = 'ko-KR';
		}

		return locale;
	}
});

mainTodayClose = function (closeId) {
	$.cookie('popup_' + closeId,'Y',{expires:1,path:'/'});
	$("#popup_" + closeId).hide();
};

mainPopupClose = function (closeId) {
	$("#popup_" + closeId).hide();
};

getCookieMain = function (name){
	var nameOfCookie = name + "=";
	var x = 0;
	while ( x <= document.cookie.length ){
		var y = (x+nameOfCookie.length);
		if ( document.cookie.substring( x, y ) == nameOfCookie ) {
			if ( (endOfCookie=document.cookie.indexOf( ";", y )) == -1 )
				endOfCookie = document.cookie.length;
			return unescape( document.cookie.substring( y, endOfCookie ) );
		}
		x = document.cookie.indexOf( " ", x ) + 1;
		if ( x == 0 )
			break;
	}
	return "";
}

//挫  臁绊
function getMainLayerPopup() {
	
			var url = '/main/ajaxLayerPopup.ssg';
		
	$.ajax({
		type : "GET",
		url : url,
		dataType : "html",
		success:function(html) {
			var $tempDiv = $('<div/>').html(html);
			// 旮搓瓿奠  胳 瓴办
			$tempDiv.find('.cmnotipop').each(function(idx, data) {
				var popupId = $(data).attr('id');

				if (getCookieMain(popupId) != "Y") {
					$("#cmmain_notipop_inr_div").append(data);
				}
			});
			// 挫  胳 瓴办
			$tempDiv.find('.notice_lpop').each(function(idx, data) {
				var popupId = $(data).attr('id');

				if (getCookieMain(popupId) != "Y") {
					$("#cmmain_notipop_inr_div").append(data);
				}
			});
			
		}
	});
}

function setSsgMainBirthDayBanr(paramObj) {
	var userBirthdayInfo = [{
		Name: paramObj.name,
		Month: paramObj.month,
		Day: paramObj.day
	}];

	if (!$('#_ssgmainTopSlide ').length) {
		return;
	}

	$.ajax({
		url: "/main/ajaxGetMainVvipBirthBanr.ssg",
		method: "POST",
		dataType: "json"
	}).done(function (data) {
		if (data.resultCode == "success") {
			$.template('tplSlideBirthday', data.result.htmlCntt);
			$.tmpl('tplSlideBirthday', userBirthdayInfo).prependTo('#_ssgmainTopSlide .ssgmain_topslide_list');

			oSsgViewMainTopThemeSlider.reloadSlider();
		}
	});
}

function getMoreContents(btnEl, domId) {
	if($('#pnshop_more_loading').is(":visible")) return;

	var domEl = $("#" + domId);
	var page = $(btnEl).data('listPage');

	var param = '';
	if(location.search) {
		param = location.search + '&page=' + page;
	} else {
		param = '?page=' + page;
	}

	$('#pnshop_more_loading').show();
	$('#main_appendMoreArea > .ssgmain_theme_more').hide();

	$.ajax({
		url: '/main/ajaxGetMoreContents.ssg' + param,
		method: 'GET',
		dataType: 'html'
	}).done(function (data) {
		
		$('#pnshop_more_loading').hide();
		
		domEl.append(data);
		domEl.append($('#main_appendMoreArea > .ssgmain_theme_more'));

		$(btnEl).data("listPage", page + 1)
				.attr("data-list-page", page + 1);
		if(true === domEl.find('.ssgmain_subject').last().data('hasNext')) {
			$('#main_appendMoreArea > .ssgmain_theme_more').show();
		}

		Clip.readyClipBtn();
		SsgStore.commit(domId, domEl.html());
	});
}

function getClipContents() {
	$.ajax({
		url: '/main/ajaxClipContents.ssg',
		method: 'GET',
		dataType: 'html'
	}).done(function (data) {
		$('#main_clipArea').append(data).show();
	});
}

function getGiftSvcItem(cmptDispCtgId) {
	var param = {
		cmptDispCtgId : cmptDispCtgId
	};

	$('#giftsvc_item_area').html('<div class="ssgmain_theme_loading"><span class="blind"> 搿 欷</span></div>');

	$.ajax({
		url: '/main/ajaxGiftSvcItem.ssg' + location.search,
		data: param,
		method: 'GET',
		dataType: 'html'
	}).done(function (data) {
		$('#giftsvc_item_area').html(data);
		Clip.readyClipBtn();
		SsgStore.commit('giftsvc_cate_area', $('#giftsvc_cate_area').html());
		SsgStore.commit('giftsvc_item_area', $('#giftsvc_item_area').html());
	});
}

function getRltimeSrchwdItemDataInit(accumDt, accumDgr, rltimeBestAccumTypeCd, siteNo, dispCtgZoneId, page) {
	$('#bestSrchwdArea').html('<div class="ssgmain_theme_loading"><span class="blind">毵 搿 欷</span></div>');

}

function getRltimeSrchwdItemData(accumDt, accumDgr, rltimeBestAccumTypeCd, siteNo, dispCtgZoneId, page) {

	$.ajax({
		url		 : '/main/ajaxRltimeBestSrchwd.ssg' + location.search,
		method	  : 'GET',
		dataType	: 'html',
		data : {accumDt : accumDt, accumDgr : accumDgr, rltimeBestAccumTypeCd : rltimeBestAccumTypeCd, siteNo : siteNo, dispCtgZoneId : dispCtgZoneId, page : page },
		success	 : function(data, status, xhr){
			$('#bestSrchwdArea').html(data);

		    if(ssg.util.hasElement('.ssgmain_rank_keyword')){
		        var oSsgViewMainrankTabs = new ssg.View.main.tabMenu({
		            sTarget: '.ssgmain_rank_keyword',
					sTabSelector: '.rank_tab_btn',
					sTabBoxSelector: '.rank_tab_panel'
		        });
		    }

		    if(ssg.util.hasElement('.rank_tab_cont')){
		        var oSsgViewMainrankTabs = new ssg.View.main.tabMenu({
		            sTarget: '.rank_tab_cont',
					sTabSelector: '.srank_tab_btn',
					sTabBoxSelector: '.ssg_cont_panel'
		        });
		    }
		    
		    $('.rank_flip').flip({
		        triggerEvent: 'click, mouseover, focusin',
		        autoStart: true,
		        autoMapping: true
		    });
		    
			Clip.readyClipBtn();
		}
	});
}

function getRltimeBestMoreItem(btnObj, btnType) {

	var $itemDiv = $(btnObj).closest('div.rank_nowbest_cont');

	if($itemDiv.find('.bx_pro_cont > ul').length == 1) {
		$.ajax({
			url		 : '/main/ajaxRltimeBestMoreItem.ssg' + location.search,
			method	  : 'GET',
			dataType	: 'html',
			data : { 
			     accumDt : $itemDiv.data('accumdt')
			   , accumDgr : $itemDiv.data('accumdgr')
			   , srchwd : encodeURIComponent($itemDiv.data('srchwd'))
			   , srchwdBestTypeCd : $itemDiv.data('typecd')
			   , siteNo : $itemDiv.data('siteno')
			   , dispCtgZoneId : $itemDiv.data('zoneid') 
			},
			success	 : function(data, status, xhr){
				if(data) {
					$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_prev').show();
					$itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul.on').removeClass('on').hide();
					$itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont').append(data);
					if($itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul').length <= 2) {
						$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_next').hide();
					}
				} else {
					$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_next').hide();
				}
				
				Clip.readyClipBtn();
			}
		});
	} else {
		if(btnType == 'prev') {
			$itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul.on').removeClass('on').hide().prev('ul').addClass('on').show();
		} else {
			$itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul.on').removeClass('on').hide().next('ul').addClass('on').show();			
		}

		if($itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul.on').prev('ul').length == 0) {
			$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_prev').hide('ul');
		} else {
			$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_prev').show('ul');
		}
		
		if($itemDiv.find('div.bx_pro_cont > ul.on').next('ul').length == 0) {
			$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_next').hide('ul');
		} else {
			$itemDiv.find('button.rank_pro_next').show('ul');
		}
	}
}

function getRltimeOrdItemData(rltimeBestAccumTypeCd, siteNo, dispCtgZoneId) {

	$('#bestOrdArea').html('<div class="ssgmain_theme_loading"><span class="blind">毵 搿 欷</span></div>');

	$.ajax({
		url		 : '/main/ajaxRltimeBestOrd.ssg' + location.search,
		method	  : 'GET',
		dataType	: 'html',
		data : { rltimeBestAccumTypeCd : rltimeBestAccumTypeCd, siteNo : siteNo, dispCtgZoneId : dispCtgZoneId },
		success	 : function(data, status, xhr){
			$('#bestOrdArea').html(data);

		    if(ssg.util.hasElement('.ssgmain_rank_order')){
		        var oSsgViewMainrankTabs = new ssg.View.main.tabMenu({
		            sTarget: '.ssgmain_rank_order',
					sTabSelector: '.rank_tab_btn',
					sTabBoxSelector: '.rank_tab_panel'
		        });
		    }
			
		    var oSsgViewMainMoreCont = new ssg.View.main.moreCont();
		    
			Clip.readyClipBtn();
		}
	});
}

			url		 : '/main/ajaxMondayMoon.ssg' + location.search,
			method	  : 'GET',
			dataType	: 'html',
			success	 : function(data, status, xhr){
				$('#mondayMoon').html(data);
				Clip.readyClipBtn();
			}
		});
	}
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var talkNavigator = {
	goSellerTalk: function(sellerhomeId, isMobile) {
        var _isMobile = (isMobile !== undefined)? isMobile : settings.isMobile;
        var dvicDivCd = _isMobile ? '20' : '10';
		var url = 'http://talk.ssg.com/webchat?sellerhomeId=' + ((sellerhomeId && sellerhomeId != 'null' && sellerhomeId != 'undefined')? $.trim(sellerhomeId) : '') + '&siteNo=' + settings.curr_siteno + '&dvicDivCd=' + dvicDivCd + '&gateType=seller';
		talkNavigator._go(url, isMobile);
	},
	goCsTalk: function(isMobile) {
		var url = 'http://talk.ssg.com/webchat?gateType=cs&siteNo=' + settings.curr_siteno;
		talkNavigator._go(url, isMobile);
	},
	_go: function(url, isMobile) {
		var _isMobile = (isMobile !== undefined)? isMobile : settings.isMobile;
		if(_isMobile) {
			
			mobileLogin('', url);
			
		} else {
			
			login('', function() {
				var newWindow = window.open(url, 'SSGTALK_WEB', 'width=1200,height=800,resizable=yes');
				if(newWindow && window.focus) {
					setTimeout(function() {
						newWindow.focus();
					}, 100);
				}
				setTimeout(function() {
					location.reload(true);
				}, 1000);
			});
			
		}
	}
};

var talkApiClient = {
	_processingUrls: [],
	_defaultSettings: {
		contentType: 'application/json;charset=UTF-8'
	},
	execute: function(paramSettings) {

		var beforeSendFunc = paramSettings.beforeSend;
		var successFunc = paramSettings.success;
		var errorFunc = paramSettings.error;
		var completeFunc = paramSettings.complete;

		var superSettings = {
			xhrFields: {
				withCredentials: true
			},
			beforeSend: function(xhr) {
				if ($.inArray(paramSettings.url, talkApiClient._processingUrls) >= 0) {
					xhr.abort();
				} else {
					talkApiClient._processingUrls.push(paramSettings.url);
					if (beforeSendFunc) {
						beforeSendFunc(xhr);
					}
				}
			},
			success: function(response, textStatus, jqXHR) {
				if (!response.code || response.code != '200') {
					if (window.console && typeof window.console.error === 'function') {
						window.console.error('talkApiClient - ' + response.message? response.message : textStatus);
					}
				} else {
					if (successFunc) {
						successFunc(response, textStatus, jqXHR);
					}
				}
			},
			error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
				if (window.console && typeof window.console.error === 'function') {
					window.console.error('Talk API error : ' + textStatus + '(' + jqXHR.status + ')');
				}
				if(errorFunc) {
					errorFunc(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown);
				}
			},
			complete: function(jqXHR, textStatus) {
				var index = $.inArray(paramSettings.url, talkApiClient._processingUrls);
				if (index >= 0) {
					talkApiClient._processingUrls.splice(index, 1);
				}
				if (completeFunc) {
					completeFunc(jqXHR, textStatus);
				}
			}
		};

		var ajaxSettings = $.extend({}, talkApiClient._defaultSettings, paramSettings, superSettings);
		$.ajax(ajaxSettings);
	}
};
</script><script type="text/javascript">
$(function() {
	if ($('#sky_ssgtalk').size() > 0 && skyTalkHandler) {
		skyTalkHandler.init();
	}
});

var skyTalkHandler = {
	timer: null,
	init: function() {
		$('#span_seller .cmfloating_btn').on('click', function() {
			var sellerhomeId = $('#span_seller').data('sellerhomeId');
			talkNavigator.goSellerTalk(sellerhomeId? sellerhomeId : '');
		});
		$('#span_ssgCs .cmfloating_btn').on('click', function() {
			talkNavigator.goCsTalk();
		});

		
	},
	_getBotChannelsOnLastMessage: function() {

		talkApiClient.execute({
			url: 'http://talk.ssg.com/api/users/bots/last-message-channels',
			success: function(response, textStatus, jqXHR) {

				if(response.detailCode) {
					switch(response.detailCode) {
						case '7000':
						case '400201':
						case '808':
							if(skyTalkHandler.timer) {
								clearInterval(skyTalkHandler.timer);
								skyTalkHandler.timer = null;
							}
							return;
					}
				}

				var botTypes = ['seller', 'ssgCs'];
				$.each(botTypes, function(i, botType) {

					if (response.data[botType] && response.data[botType].unread_message_count > 0) {
						var $spanBot = $('#span_' + botType);
						$spanBot.find('.cmfloating_push').html(response.data[botType].unread_message_count);
						var message = response.data[botType].last_message.message;
						if(message.length > 20) {
							message = message.substring(0, 17) + '...';
						}
						$spanBot.find('.cmfloating_msg_txt').html(message);

						if(!$spanBot.data('lastMsgTime') || $spanBot.data('lastMsgTime') < response.data[botType].last_message.created_at) {
							if (botType == 'seller') {
								$spanBot.find('.cmfloating_thmb_img img').one('error', function() {
									this.src = 'http://ui.ssgcdn.com/ui/m_ssg/img/ssgtalk_web/profile_default.png';
								}).attr('src', response.data[botType].last_message.user.profile_url);
								skySsgtalk.onPush('.cmfloating_btnseller');
							} else if (botType == 'ssgCs') {
								skySsgtalk.onPush('.cmfloating_btncsbot');
							}
							$spanBot.data('lastMsgTime', response.data[botType].last_message.created_at);
							for (var index = 0; index < response.data[botType].members.length; index++) {
								if (response.data[botType].members[index].user_id.indexOf('B') == 0) {
									$spanBot.data('sellerhomeId', response.data[botType].members[index].user_id.substring(1));
									break;
								}
							}
						}
					} else {
						if (botType == 'seller') {
							skySsgtalk.offPush('.cmfloating_btnseller');
						} else if (botType == 'ssgCs') {
							skySsgtalk.offPush('.cmfloating_btncsbot');
						}
					}
				});
			}

		});
	},
	
	createItemSellerTalk: function(sellerhomeId, itemImgUrl, singleTarget) {
		talkApiClient.execute({
			url: 'http://talk.ssg.com/api/sellerhome/' + sellerhomeId,
			success: function(response, textStatus, jqXHR) {

				$('#span_item_seller .cmfloating_btn').unbind().on('click', function() {
					if(singleTarget) {
						sellerTalkPopup(sellerhomeId, false);
					} else {
						$('#sellerTalkBtnClick').trigger('click');
					}
				});

				$('#img_item_seller_profile').one('error', function() {
					this.src = 'http://ui.ssgcdn.com/ui/m_ssg/img/ssgtalk_web/profile_default.png';
				}).attr('src', response.sellerHome.profileImageUrl);
				$('#img_item_seller_item').one('error', function() {
					this.src = 'http://img.ssgcdn.com/trans.ssg?src=/ui/ssg/img/common/img_ready_500x500.jpg&w=100&h=100&t=a1df53586ad84acdce844f0ae535a73cafe168c6';
				}).attr('src', itemImgUrl);
				$('#span_item_seller').show();

				skySsgtalk.showSellerDtl();
			},
			error: function() {
				$('#span_item_seller').hide();
			}
		});
	}
};
</script>

 <script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function() {
		bannerTimeCheck();
	});
	var mallBanrStrtDts 	= '';
	var mallBanrEndDts 		= '';
	var commBanrStrtDts 	= ''; 
	var commBanrEndDts 		= ''; 
	function bannerTimeCheck(){				
		var nowTimeNum	  =   Math.floor(new Date()/1000);
		//氇半 搿 
		if(mallBanrStrtDts.length > 0){
			var mallStartTime = new Date(mallBanrStrtDts.substring(0,4),mallBanrStrtDts.substring(4,6)-1,mallBanrStrtDts.substring(6,8),mallBanrStrtDts.substring(8,10),mallBanrStrtDts.substring(10,12),mallBanrStrtDts.substring(12));			  // 检
			var mallendTime   = new Date(mallBanrEndDts.substring(0,4),mallBanrEndDts.substring(4,6)-1,mallBanrEndDts.substring(6,8),mallBanrEndDts.substring(8,10),mallBanrEndDts.substring(10,12),mallBanrEndDts.substring(12));			  // 膦耄检
			var mallStartTimeNum	=   Math.floor(mallStartTime/1000);
			var mallendTimeNum	=   Math.floor(mallendTime/1000);
			
			if(nowTimeNum >= mallStartTimeNum && nowTimeNum <= mallendTimeNum){				
				$('#floatWrap3').show();
				floatBanner3Start();
			}
			
		}else{
			$('#floatWrap3').hide();
			$.cookie('floating_ty1', '', {expires: -1, path: '/'});
		}
		
		//瓿淀 搿 
		if(commBanrStrtDts.length > 0){
			var commStartTime = new Date(commBanrStrtDts.substring(0,4),commBanrStrtDts.substring(4,6)-1,commBanrStrtDts.substring(6,8),commBanrStrtDts.substring(8,10),commBanrStrtDts.substring(10,12),commBanrStrtDts.substring(12));			  // 检
			var commendTime = new Date(commBanrEndDts.substring(0,4),commBanrEndDts.substring(4,6)-1,commBanrEndDts.substring(6,8),commBanrEndDts.substring(8,10),commBanrEndDts.substring(10,12),commBanrEndDts.substring(12));			  // 膦耄检
			var commStartTimeNum = Math.floor(commStartTime/1000);
			var commendTimeNum = Math.floor(commendTime/1000);
			
			if(nowTimeNum >= commStartTimeNum && nowTimeNum <= commendTimeNum){				
				$('#floatWrap2').show();
				floatBanner2Start();
			}
		}else{
			$('#floatWrap2').hide();
			$.cookie('floating_ty2', '', {expires: -1, path: '/',domain:'ssg.com'});
		}
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
//觳挫 挫 甏 ろ毽巾
// #370751 [] 觳  毽ろ  觳
var Replacement = {
    getItems : function (htData) {
        return $.ajax({
            type: "get",
            dataType : "html",
            data: {
                itemId : htData.replaceCode,
                siteNo : htData.replaceSiteno,
                displayPrc : htData.replaceDisplayprc,
                sellPrc : htData.replaceSellprc
            },
            url : '/disp/list/ajaxReplaceItem'
        });
    }
};

$(function(){
    var oReplacementLayer=function(){function n(){var n=null,e=function(){n=$("#lyChange"),_welReplaceGoods=n.find(".ly_chg_goods")},l=function(){var n=_welReplaceGoods.children(),e=n.filter(".on").prev();e.length?e.addClass("on").siblings().removeClass("on"):n.last().addClass("on").siblings().removeClass("on")},o=function(){var n=_welReplaceGoods.children(),e=n.filter(".on").next();e.length?e.addClass("on").siblings().removeClass("on"):n.first().addClass("on").siblings().removeClass("on")},s=function(){n.on("click",".ly_chg_prev",l),n.on("click",".ly_chg_next",o)};return this.init=function(){return e(),s(),this},this.render=function(n){_welReplaceGoods.html(n).removeClass("loading")},this.empty=function(){_welReplaceGoods.html("").addClass("loading")},this.init()}return new n}();
    var oSsgViewLayerPopup = new ssg.View.layerPopup({
    	bGlobal  : true,
        sTarget  : '.btn_change', // 挫  氤搓赴 氩
        sClose   : '.ly_chg_close', // 挫  旮 氩
        htDefault: {
            overlayCSS: {
                backgroundColor: '#fff',
                opacity: 0.8
            },
            onOverlayClick: function() { oSsgViewLayerPopup.closeLayer(); } // overlay click 挫 旮
        },
        sNamespaceEmit: '.ssgReplaceLayer'
    });

    oSsgViewLayerPopup.on('beforeOpen.ssgReplaceLayer', function(htData){
        if(htData && htData.replaceCode){
            Replacement.getItems(htData).done(function(data){
                var trim = data.trim();
                if(trim){
	            	oReplacementLayer.render(data);
                } else {
                	alert("欷牍 觳挫 惦.");
                	oSsgViewLayerPopup.closeLayer();
                }
            });
        }
    });

    oSsgViewLayerPopup.on('afterClose.ssgReplaceLayer', function(){
        oReplacementLayer.empty();
    });
});
	
$(function(){
	//惦钒 挫
	var oSsgQuickViewLayerPopup = new ssg.View.layerPopup({
		bGlobal  : true,
		sTarget  : '.cmqv_btn_view', // 挫  氤搓赴 氩
		sClose   : '.cmqv_btn_close', // 挫  旮 氩
		htDefault: {
			overlayCSS: {
				backgroundColor: '#fff',
				opacity: 0.8
			},
            css: {
                backgroundColor: "none"
            },
			onOverlayClick: function() { oSsgQuickViewLayerPopup.closeLayer(); } // overlay click 挫 旮
		},
        sNamespaceEmit: '.ssgQuickview'
	});
 
	oSsgQuickViewLayerPopup.on('beforeOpen.ssgQuickview', function(htData){
        if(htData && htData.replaceHref){
                $('#ly_cmqv_ifr').prop('src', htData.replaceHref);
        }
    });
 
    oSsgQuickViewLayerPopup.on('beforeClose.ssgQuickview', function(htData){
    	$('#ly_cmqv_ifr').contents().find('body').empty();
        $('#ly_cmqv_ifr').prop('src', '');
    });
	
	//  挫
	var oSsgViewTalkLayerPopup = new ssg.View.layerPopup({
		sTarget  : '.cdtl_lypop_open', // 挫  氤搓赴 氩
		sClose   : '.ly_close', // 挫  旮 氩
		htDefault: {
			overlayCSS: {
				backgroundColor: '#000',
				opacity: 0.7
			},
			css: {
				backgroundColor: "none"
			},
			onOverlayClick: function() { oSsgViewTalkLayerPopup.closeLayer(); } // overlay click 挫 旮
		}
	});

    //  错挫
    $('.cdtl_ly_talk .cdtl_ly_close').on('click', function(e){
        $('.cdtl_ly_talk').removeClass('on');
    });
	
	var welLayerPopup = $('.cdtl_lypop_wrap');
	welLayerPopup.on('change', '.custom_rdo input[type=radio]', function(){
		var sRadioGroupName = $(this).attr('name');
		var welRadioGroup = $('input[type=radio][name='+sRadioGroupName+']');
		
		welRadioGroup.each(function(){
			$(this).parent('.custom_rdo').toggleClass('on', $(this).is(':checked'));
		});
	});

	//  搿攴胳 
	$('#sellerTalkQnaClick, #sellerTalkBtnClick, #sellerTalkOptBarClick').on('click', function(){
      if (UserInfo.isLoginYn == "N") {
        login('', function(){
          $.cookie('ITEM_VIEW_SELLERTALK_LAYER', 'pc');
          document.location.reload();
        });
        return;
      }
      oSsgViewTalkLayerPopup.showByTarget('#cdtl_lypop_talk');
    });

    // ID  , 茧┐ 氚搿 ろ
    var talkId = $.cookie('ITEM_VIEW_SELLERTALK_ID');
    if(!!talkId){
      $.cookie('ITEM_VIEW_SELLERTALK_ID', '');
      if (UserInfo.isLoginYn !== "N") {
        sellerTalkPopup(talkId);
      }
    }

    // PC  挫
    var layerYn = $.cookie('ITEM_VIEW_SELLERTALK_LAYER');
    if(layerYn === 'pc'){
      $.cookie('ITEM_VIEW_SELLERTALK_LAYER', '');
      if (UserInfo.isLoginYn !== "N") {
        $('#sellerTalkBtnClick').trigger('click');
      }
    }
});
